//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = p1a & p1b & p1c | p1a & p1b & p1d | p1a & p1c & p1d | p1b & p1c & p1d;
    assign p2y = p2a & p2b & p2c | p2a & p2b & p2d | p2a & p2c & p2d | p2b & p2c & p2d;

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = (p1a & p1b & p1c) | (p1a & p1b & p1d) | (p1a & p1c & p1d) | (p1a & p1b & p2a & p2b) | (p1a & p1b & p2a & p2c) | (p1a & p1b & p2a & p2d) | (p1a & p1b & p2b & p2c) | (p1a & p1b & p2b & p2d) | (p1a & p1c & p2a & p2c) | (p1a & p1c & p2a & p2d) | (p1a & p1c & p2b & p2d) | (p1b & p1c & p2a & p2b) | (p1b & p1c & p2a & p2c) | (p1b & p1c & p2a & p2d) | (p1b & p1d & p2a & p2b) | (p1b & p1d & p2a & p2c) | (p1b & p1d & p2a & p2d) | (p1c & p1d & p2a & p2b) | (p1c & p1d & p2b & p2c) | (p1c & p1d & p2b & p2d) | (p1c & p1d & p2a & p2c) | (p1c & p1d & p2a & p2d) | (p1d & p2a & p2b & p2c) | (p1d & p2a & p2b & p2d);
    assign p2y = (p2a & p2b & p2c) | (p2a & p2b & p2d) | (p2a & p2c & p2d) | (p2a & p2b & p1a & p1b) | (p2a & p2b & p1a & p1c) | (p2a & p2b & p1a & p1d) | (p2a & p2b & p1b & p1d) | (p2a & p2c & p1a & p1b) | (p2a & p2c & p1a & p1c) | (p2a & p2c & p1a & p1d) | (p2a & p2c & p1b & p1d) | (p2a & p2d & p1a & p1b) | (p2a & p2d & p1a & p1c) | (p2a & p2d & p1a & p1d) | (p2a & p2d & p1b & p1d) | (p2b & p2c & p1a & p1b) | (p2b & p2c & p1a & p1c) | (p2b & p2c & p1a & p1d) | (p2b & p2c & p1b & p1d) | (p2b & p2d & p1a & p1b) | (p2b & p2d & p1a & p1c) | (p2b & p2d & p1a & p1d) | (p2b & p2d & p1b & p1d) | (p2c & p2d & p1a & p1b) | (p2c & p2d & p1a & p1c) | (p2c & p2d & p1a & p1d) | (p2c & p2d & p1b & p1d);

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    wire w1, w2, w3, w4;
    assign w1 = p1a & p1b & p1c;
    assign w2 = p1a & p1b & p1d;
    assign w3 = p1a & p1c & p1d;
    assign w4 = p1b & p1c & p1d;
    assign p1y = w1 | w2 | w3 | w4;

    assign w5 = p2a & p2b & p2c;
    assign w6 = p2a & p2b & p2d;
    assign w7 = p2a & p2c & p2d;
    assign w8 = p2b & p2c & p2d;
    assign p2y = w5 | w6 | w7 | w8;

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = p1a & p1b & p1c | p1a & p1b & p1d | p1a & p1c & p1d | p1b & p1c & p1d;
    assign p2y = p2a & p2b & p2c | p2a & p2b & p2d | p2a & p2c & p2d | p2b & p2c & p2d;

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );	

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );
    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);
endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule

//The 7400-series integrated circuits are a series of digital chips with a few gates each. 
//The 7420 is a chip with two 4-input NAND gates.

// Create a module with the same functionality as the 7420 chip. It has 8 inputs and 2 outputs.

//Hint: You need to drive two signals (p1y and p2y) with a value.

module top_module ( 
    input p1a, p1b, p1c, p1d,
    output p1y,
    input p2a, p2b, p2c, p2d,
    output p2y );

    assign p1y = ~(p1a & p1b & p1c & p1d);
    assign p2y = ~(p2a & p2b & p2c & p2d);

endmodule
